           To achieve `receivedanalysis`, a rover needs to `sample_rock` and then `send_analysis`. This requires the rover to be `above` the rock, have a `free` store, and the ray not to be `blocked`.
           
           We need to:
           - Get `receivedimage` for `v17`, `v18`, `v19` with `v11` (mode).
           - Get `receivedanalysis` for a rock of `type` `v2` (e.g., `v1` or `v4`).
           - Get `receivedanalysis` for a rock of `type` `v6` (e.g., `v5`, `v7` or `v8`).
           
           Let's use rover `v12` for imaging and rover `v14` for sampling.
           
           For `receivedimage`:
           - `calibrate` camera `v10` on `v12` at `#o3` for `v17`.
           - `take_image` of `v17` by `v12` at `#o3` with `v10` and `v11`.
           - `send_image` of `v17` by `v12` at `#o0` to `v9`.
           - Repeat for `v18` and `v19`.
           
           For `receivedanalysis`:
           - `sample_rock` (type `v2`) by `v14` at `#o5` (e.g., `v1`).
           - `send_analysis` of `v1` by `v14` at `#o0` to `v9`.
           - `sample_rock` (type `v6`) by `v14` at `#o5` (e.g., `v5`).
           - `send_analysis` of `v5` by `v14` at `#o0` to `v9`.
           
           It's important to move the rover to the correct configurations for each action, or use existing `atconf` if they satisfy the conditions.
           Rover `v12` is at `v13`. We need to move it to `#o3` for `calibrate` and `take_image`, and to `#o0` for `send_image`.
           Rover `v14` is at `v15`. We need to move it to `#o5` for `sample_rock`, and to `#o0` for `send_analysis`.
           
           The plan will involve a sequence of calibrations, image captures, image transmissions, rock samplings, and analysis transmissions.
           
           --Plan--:
           (calibrate v12 #o3 #o4 v17 v10)
           (take_image v12 #o3 #o4 v17 v10 v11)
           (move v12 #o3 #o2 #o0)
           (send_image v12 #o0 #o1 v9 v17 v11)
           (move v12 #o0 #o2 #o3)
           (calibrate v12 #o3 #o4 v18 v10)
           (take_image v12 #o3 #o4 v18 v10 v11)
           (move v12 #o3 #o2 #o0)
           (send_image v12 #o0 #o1 v9 v18 v11)
           (move v12 #o0 #o2 #o3)
           (calibrate v12 #o3 #o4 v19 v10)
           (take_image v12 #o3 #o4 v19 v10 v11)
           (move v12 #o3 #o2 #o0)
           (send_image v12 #o0 #o1 v9 v19 v11)
           (move v14 v15 #o2 #o5)
           (sample_rock v14 #o5 v1 v16)
           (move v14 #o5 #o2 #o0)
           (send_analysis v14 #o0 #o1 v9 v1)
           (move v14 #o0 #o2 #o5)
           (sample_rock v14 #o5 v5 v16)
           (move v14 #o5 #o2 #o0)
           (send_analysis v14 #o0 #o1 v9 v5)
           
           --Configurations--:
           (#o3 v12 #o4 v17): (1.0, 1.0)
           (#o0 v12 #o1 v9): (0.0, 0.0)
           (#o3 v12 #o4 v18): (1.0, 1.0)
           (#o3 v12 #o4 v19): (1.0, 1.0)
           (#o5 v14 #o4 v1): (-1.0, 1.0)
           (#o0 v14 #o1 v9): (0.0, 0.0)
